## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: classical mechanics (nonlinear oscillations / dynamical systems)
**Analysis**: The variables x (position), v (velocity), and dv_dt (acceleration) indicate a second-order ODE written as a first-order system for an oscillator. Typical relationships are restoring forces depending on x (often odd/nonlinear) plus damping depending on v and possible external/parametric forcing depending on t.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Kinematic identity (state-space form): dx_dt = v (linking position and velocity in oscillator ODEs)
- Linear harmonic oscillator (undamped): dv_dt = -c0 * x (Hooke restoring force per unit mass)
- Linear damped oscillator: dv_dt = -c0 * x - c1 * v (viscous damping proportional to velocity)
- Shifted equilibrium oscillator: dv_dt = -c0 * (x - c1) - c2 * v (oscillation about nonzero equilibrium)
- Quadratic drag damping: dv_dt = -c0 * x - c1 * v * Abs(v) (aerodynamic-like damping at higher speeds)
- Coulomb (dry) friction damping: dv_dt = -c0 * x - c1 * sign(v) (piecewise-constant friction opposing motion)
- Duffing oscillator (softening/hardening spring): dv_dt = -c0 * x - c1 * x**3 - c2 * v (cubic stiffness nonlinearity)
- General polynomial restoring force: dv_dt = -(c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * x**5) - c3 * v (higher-order nonlinear stiffness)
- Nonlinear damping (Rayleigh-type): dv_dt = -c0 * x - (c1 * v + c2 * v**3) (damping increases with speed magnitude)
- Van der Pol oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * (c1 - c2 * x**2) * v - c3 * x (negative damping at small |x|, limit cycle)
- Pendulum small-to-large angle (with damping): dv_dt = -c0 * sin(c1 * x) - c2 * v (geometric nonlinearity in restoring torque)
- Forced oscillator (additive drive): dv_dt = -c0 * x - c1 * v + c2 * cos(c3 * t) (external periodic forcing)
- Parametrically excited oscillator: dv_dt = -(c0 + c1 * cos(c2 * t)) * x - c3 * v (time-varying stiffness, Mathieu-like)
- Nonlinear forced Duffing: dv_dt = -c0 * x - c1 * x**3 - c2 * v + c3 * cos(c4 * t) (nonlinear resonance/chaos regimes)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Conservative oscillator signature: dv_dt depends on x but not on v (no damping) → energy approximately conserved; trajectories form closed curves in (x, v).
- Viscous damping signature: linear -c * v term → exponential decay of oscillation envelope; phase portrait spirals into equilibrium.
- Dry friction signature: term proportional to sign(v) → stick-slip and non-smooth dynamics; acceleration jumps at v = 0.
- Quadratic/aerodynamic damping signature: v * Abs(v) term → stronger damping at high speed; decay rate depends on amplitude.
- Nonlinear stiffness signature: odd powers of x (x**3, x**5) → amplitude-dependent frequency (hardening/softening backbone curve).
- Geometric restoring force signature: sin(c * x) in dv_dt → bounded restoring force; near-separatrix behavior and period growth near large amplitudes.
- Self-excited oscillation signature: (c0 - c1 * x**2) * v term → negative damping at small amplitude and positive at large, producing a stable limit cycle.
- External forcing signature: additive cos(c * t) or sin(c * t) → entrainment, resonance peaks, and possible quasiperiodic/chaotic responses when combined with nonlinearity.
- Parametric excitation signature: (c0 + c1 * cos(c2 * t)) * x term → instability tongues (Mathieu-type) and parametric resonance when drive frequency relates to natural frequency.

Best expression     : c0*x + c1*v + c2*sin(c3*t + c4)
Structure desc      : The formula is an additive combination of two linear terms in x and v plus a sinusoidal term in t: c0*x + c1*v + c2*sin(c3*t+c4). With fitted values, the behavior is dominated by the linear components (−3.506·x and −0.718·v), while the sinusoid is a small modulation of amplitude 0.094 with near-unit angular frequency (c3≈1.002) and phase c4≈6.166 (≈2π−0.118). Thus it is approximately equivalent to y ≈ −3.506x − 0.718v + 0.094·sin(t + 6.166), i.e., a mainly linear model with a weak periodic ripple; the low NMSE indicates this structure fits well.
Fitted params       : c0=-3.5060e+00, c1=-7.1831e-01, c2=9.3955e-02, c3=1.0020e+00, c4=6.1657e+00
Train NMSE          : 2.59e-03
Test NMSE           : 2.51e-03
OOD Test NMSE       : 3.07e-02

GT: F0*sin(t) - beta*sin(v) - omega0**c0*(gamma*Abs(v)**c1 + c2)*x
Candidate formulas: 299

GT (fixed function):
\[
-3.4278620084\,x\big(0.03499775369\,|v|^{1/3}+1\big)+0.1002992557\sin(t)-0.8884946707\sin(v)
\]
Key structural requirements:
- Has **both** \(\sin(t)\) and \(\sin(v)\) terms (separable: one depends only on \(t\), one only on \(v\)).
- Has an \(x\)-term whose coefficient depends on \(v\) via \(|v|^{1/3}\): specifically \(-A x - B x|v|^{1/3}\).
- Uses **Abs(v)** with exponent \(1/3\); cannot be replaced by \(v\) globally (since \(v\) can be negative).

Now check candidates (grouping by why they fail; any candidate not containing the needed functional forms cannot be made equivalent by tuning constants).

1. `c0*x + c1*v + c2*sin(c3*t + c4)`  
   Has \(\sin(t)\) (via phase/frequency), but **no \(\sin(v)\)** and **no \(x|v|^{1/3}\)**. Cannot match.

2. Polynomial/rational in \(t\), no trig in \(v\), no \(|v|^{1/3}\). Cannot.

3. Adds \(x\cos(c6 t)\): still no \(\sin(v)\), no \(|v|^{1/3}\). Cannot.

4–6. Contain \(x\cos(c t)\) and algebraic/rational pieces; **no \(\sin(t)\) and \(\sin(v)\) simultaneously**, and no \(|v|^{1/3}\) in an \(x\)-multiplier. Cannot.

7–8. Pure algebraic in \(x,v\). No trig. Cannot.

9. `... + c2*sin(c3*v + c4) + c5*x*cos(c6*t)`  
   Can create a \(\sin(v)\) term, and an \(x\cos(\cdot t)\) term, but GT needs **\(\sin(t)\)** (not multiplied by \(x\)) and needs \(x(1+|v|^{1/3})\). This has neither separable \(\sin(t)\) nor \(|v|^{1/3}\). Cannot.

10–23. Various \(x\cos(t)\), logs/exp; none provide both \(\sin(t)\) and \(\sin(v)\) plus \(x|v|^{1/3}\). Cannot.

24. Has \(\sin(c3 x+c4)\) (wrong variable), not \(\sin(t)\) or \(\sin(v)\) as required. Cannot.

25–29. Algebraic couplings, no correct trig pair and no \(|v|^{1/3}\) in the \(x\)-coefficient. Cannot.

30–38. Polynomial variants; no \(\sin(t)\) and \(\sin(v)\) pair, no \(|v|^{1/3}\). Cannot.

39–40. Have \(\log(|v|+1)\sin(\cdot)\) with sine depending on \(x\) (and possibly \(v\)); GT needs a **pure** \(\sin(v)\) term and a **pure** \(\sin(t)\) term. Not possible.

41–88. Mostly polynomials plus \(x\cos(t)\), \( \cos(t)\), logs/exp in \(t\) or \(v\); none contain \(|v|^{1/3}\) multiplied by \(x\) and also both \(\sin(t)\) and \(\sin(v)\). Cannot.

   Can make a \(\sin(t)\) term but it is multiplied by \(x^{c3}\); GT’s \(\sin(t)\) is **additive and independent of \(x\)**. Setting \(c2=0\) removes it, but then no \(\sin(t)\). Cannot.

109. \(v\cos(t)|v|\): wrong dependence; no \(\sin(t)\), no \(\sin(v)\). Cannot.

110. Logistic/exp in \(v\) plus linear in \(x\); no required trig/abs-power. Cannot.

117–119. Algebraic; no trig pair and no \(|v|^{1/3}\). Cannot.

   Can match \(\sin(v)\) (choose \(c3=1,c4=0,c2=-0.88849\)), but has **no \(\sin(t)\)** and no \(x|v|^{1/3}\). Cannot.

121–145. Variants with \(x\cos(t)\), rationals, logs, etc. None include \(|v|^{1/3}\) in the coefficient of \(x\), and none simultaneously provide separable \(\sin(t)\) and \(\sin(v)\) (some provide one sine but not both). Cannot.

Crucial impossibility across the entire list:
- **No candidate contains an \(x\cdot |v|^{1/3}\) term (or any tunable mechanism to produce exactly \(|v|^{1/3}\) multiplying \(x\))**.
- Candidates that include \(\sin(t)\) never also include \(\sin(v)\) *and* the required \(x(1+k|v|^{1/3})\) damping form.
